Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Treplus Communities contact form
URLhttps://www.trepluscommunities.com/contact
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/24
Score1363
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1363, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 307. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 600. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 98

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 84 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 29 (Element has insufficient color contrast)

Issue imageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 60

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r2, score 32 (Image has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test image-alt, score 32 (Image has no text alternative)
  • Package continuum, test 89, score 32 (img element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 56

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 52 (Non-underlined adjacent links)
  • Package alfa, test r62, score 4 (Inline link is not distinct from the surrounding text except by color)
  • Package axe, test link-in-text-block, score 2 (Link is not distinct from surrounding text without reliance on color)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 50

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 28 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test link-name, score 21 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 28 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 32

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 26 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 9 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))

Issue tabFocusability

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 27

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focAll, score 25 (Discrepancy between elements that should be and that are Tab-focusable)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 17

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 14 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 2 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)

Issue roleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 13

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test role, score 11 (Nonexistent or implicit-overriding role)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 10

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 8 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)

Issue autocompleteBad

WCAG: 1.3.5

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test autocomplete, score 6 (Name or email input is missing its required autocomplete attribute)

Issue leadingInsufficient

WCAG: 1.4.8

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r73, score 6 (Paragraph of text has insufficient line height)

Issue fontSizeAbsolute

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r74, score 6 (Paragraph text has an absolute font size)

Issue leadingAbsolute

WCAG: 1.4.12

Score: 8

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r80, score 6 (Paragraph text has an absolute line height)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 7

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 3 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 4 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue textAreaNoText

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 6

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 872, score 4 (textarea element has no accessible name, but only a placeholder attribute)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 5

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 3 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue fontSmall

WCAG: 1.4

Score: 5

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r75, score 3 (Font size is smaller than 9 pixels)

Issue controlLabelInvisible

WCAG: 2.4.6

Score: 5

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test label-title-only, score 3 (Form element has no visible label)

Issue inputOnlyPlaceholder

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 5

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 863, score 3 (input has an accessible name that depends on a placeholder)

Issue focusableOperable

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 4

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focOp, score 2 (Operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

Issue inconsistentStyles

WCAG: 3.2.4

Score: 4

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test styleDiff, score 2 (Heading, link, and button style inconsistencies)

Issue zIndexNotZero

WCAG: 1.4

Score: 4

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test zIndex, score 2 (Layering with nondefault z-index values)

Issue decorativeElementExposed

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 4

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r86, score 2 (Element marked as decorative is in the accessibility tree or has no none/presentation role)

Issue repeatedContentRisk

WCAG: 2.4.1

Score: 3

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r87, score 1 (First focusable element is not a link to the main content)

Issue frameContentRisk

WCAG: 4.1

Score: 3

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test frame-tested, score 1 (Some content is in an iframe and therefore may not be testable for accessibility)

Issue hiddenContentRisk

WCAG: 4.1

Score: 3

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test hidden-content, score 1 (Some content is hidden and therefore may not be testable for accessibility)

Issue linkConfusionRisk

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 3

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test identical-links-same-purpose, score 1 (Links with the same accessible name may serve dissimilar purposes)
